# Amazon Top 10K Rich Persona Reviewer IDs

This file stores a reusable reviewer queue for staged Amazon review persona inference. It only contains reviewer IDs and lightweight selection context, so teammates can retrieve the corresponding review histories from the indexed Amazon artifacts later.

## Source Pool

- Dataset artifact: `MatrAIx/MatrAIx/amazon/modal_artifacts/amazon_reviews_2018_2023_eligible_users_min30_verified70_text2000`
- Time window: `2018-2023`
- Source eligibility: `review_count >= 30`, `verified_share >= 0.70`, `text_chars >= 2000`
- Eligible users considered: `1,744,018`
- Selected reviewer IDs: `10,000`

## Ranking Logic

The IDs are ranked by a rich-persona score intended to prioritize users likely to yield informative persona representations. The score uses percentile ranks over text volume, text-review count, category breadth, history length, review count, and verified-purchase share. History length is recomputed from `first_date` and `last_date` when needed.

| Signal | Weight |
|---|---:|
| `text_chars` | 0.35 |
| `text_reviews` | 0.20 |
| `category_count` | 0.20 |
| `history_days` | 0.15 |
| `review_count` | 0.05 |
| `verified_share` | 0.05 |
